We give thanks and pray over every single bean, knowing it has been nurtured by God's grace.

"In the same way, let your light shine before others, that they may see your good deeds and glorify your Father in heaven." 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 Matthew 5:16

OR Church and Coffee has no affiliation with Jehovah's Witnesses, the Unification Church, the Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints, Quompa, or Talappan (Gospel Missionary Church / Remnant Academy).

Church
A Time of Rest and Peace in God's Love

Worship & Networking

Let us worship together and give thanks for the daily blessings God gives us in fellowship. After worship, through connecting with one another, we hope to encourage each other and grow deeper in relationship.

We also open our space for praise gatherings and various events organized by ministries. If you have a vision or idea you'd like to see come to life, please feel free to reach out.

Vision
The 7 Essentials of the Church

The "7 Essentials of the Church" put forward by JCMN were drawn up in 2000 when church leaders from around the world gathered to discuss what a biblically grounded church looks like. Focused on "essentials" rather than methods, these principles serve as a powerful foundation for many believers 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 a guide for the church to grow as a life-filled community.

"Kasa no Ie de Nete" 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 a Japanese mnemonic for remembering all 7 essentials

Relationships

Deepening with God and connecting as His family. In our worship, each person comes before God just as they are, building a deeper relationship with Him and with one another through prayer.

Participation

The joy of serving together. "Offer your bodies as a living sacrifice, holy and pleasing to God." (Romans 12:1). Through service, our very being is opened toward God.

Empowerment

Using gifts in faith. God entrusts each person with a calling. Rather than burying our gifts, we seek to be vessels that share them in faith and build up those around us.

Jesus-Centred

True freedom and peace. "I no longer live, but Christ lives in me." (Galatians 2:20). We seek to be a church where the Holy Spirit moves 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 centred entirely on Jesus.

Evangelism & Multiplication

A delivery of love. Living as "the light of the world and the salt of the earth" is a delivery of love born through the work of the Holy Spirit. We cherish a deep love for every soul that is saved.

Networks

Connection between churches. "The whole body, joined and held together by every supporting ligament, grows and builds itself up in love." (Ephesians 4:16). We pray for churches to support one another and extend God's kingdom.

Adaptable Structures

Flexibility nurtures life. OR Church actively embraces personal worship, online worship, and small-group fellowship to meet the needs of an urban lifestyle. Following Jesus' teaching 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 "new wine into new wineskins" 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 we believe that a flexible structure will allow OR Church to grow as a life-filled church.

COFFEE

A moment of grace

Roast
Coffee Roasting & a Moment of Grace
"So then, whether you eat or drink or whatever you do, do everything for the glory of God." 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 1 Corinthians 10:31

At OR Church and Coffee, we roast green beans slowly just for you. In about 10脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聯15 minutes, your aromatic coffee is ready.

The roaster carefully selects and prayerfully roasts each special coffee for you. Every bean carries the grace of God and the stories of the people who grew it.

The roaster will share the origin of the beans, the people behind them, and the story of each farm 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 all while roasting your very own batch.

Food Hygiene License No.: 3553708

Chill & Relax

OR Church and Coffee is a place where you can spend time however you like. While waiting for your roast, enjoy a tasting and take a moment to rest your heart.

New friendships, deepening faith, and aromatic coffee 脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聝脙聝脗聜脙聜脗垄脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聙脙聝脗聝脙聜脗聜脙聝脗聜脙聜脗聰 experience the love of God in every visit.

Directions

Walking directions from Yahiro Station (South Exit)

1

Exit through the ticket gates and turn left.

2

Take the stairs down to the South Exit.

3

Once outside, head diagonally to the left.

4

Continue straight ahead.

5

When you reach the main road, turn left.

6

Continue straight ahead.

7

Turn right and cross at the pedestrian crossing.

8

Turn right and continue straight ahead.

9

Turn left.

10

Continue straight ahead.

11

Head diagonally to the right.

12

Continue straight ahead.

13

Turn left and continue straight ahead.

14

Continue straight along the road on the left.

15

The cream-colored building next to the utility pole on the right is the church.

16

The exterior wall is designed in the image of "the blood of Jesus."

17

You have arrived at the church!
